name:Y‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçm‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Business Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:32 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:I stayed in Xueye Ruju and Xueye Weisheng hotels consecutively. These two hotels have their own characteristics. Let's review them together.
1. Hotel room: Ruju is one level higher than Weisheng. Ruju is newly decorated and fully equipped, while Weisheng's room has a musty smell;
2. Public facilities: The two hotels are equally good and each has its own characteristics. Weisheng is slightly better, and the gym and swimming pool are similar; Ruju has slightly better children's facilities, while Weisheng is next to the lake and has a large garden; Weisheng has an underground parking lot, while Ruju has to run a long way to park.
3. Meals: Weisheng is much better than Ruju, cheaper and more delicious.
4. Service: Each has its own advantages and disadvantages. Weisheng only gives two bottles of water, and you have to pay more or get a miscellaneous brand of water. Ruju gives 4 bottles of water and there are free drinks in the lobby.
Overall, if young couples are suitable for Ruju, Weisheng is suitable for family travel. I give Ruju 4 points and Weisheng 4.5; these two hotels are considered good in the local area, but of course they are not a little bit worse than Sanya hotels.
